List<Map<String, Object>> res  = new ArrayList<>();
		List<MessageDto> messageDtoList = new ArrayList<>();
		//开始时间
		Date starDate = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd").parse(date);
		//本月第一天
		String beginDateOfMonth = DateUtils.getBeginDateOfMonth(starDate);
		//结束时间
		String endDate  = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd").format(DateUtils.addDate(starDate,1L));
		List<MessageDto> orders = orderDao.findNotCplusOrdersByTime(date,endDate);
		if(orders.isEmpty()){
			return  res;
		}
		Map<Long, List<MessageDto>> ordersMap = orders.stream().collect(Collectors.groupingBy(MessageDto::getProductId));
		List<Long> productList = orders.stream().map(MessageDto :: getProductId).distinct().collect(Collectors.toList());
		List<Map<String, Object>> monthCountList = orderDao.findOrderCountByPIdAndDate(beginDateOfMonth,endDate, productList);
		Map<Long, Integer> monthCountMap = new HashMap<>();
		monthCountList.stream().forEach(m->{
		    Long pid = 	MapHelper.getLong(m,"product_id");
			int  monthtotal = 	MapHelper.getInt(m,"monthtotal");
			monthCountMap.put(pid,monthtotal);
		});
		for (Map.Entry<Long, List<MessageDto>> map: ordersMap.entrySet()) {
			List<String> list = new ArrayList<>();
			int monthCount= monthCountMap.containsKey(map.getKey())?monthCountMap.get(map.getKey()): Constants.ZERO;
			List<MessageDto> value = map.getValue();
			//订单量
			long successcount = value.stream().filter(Orders -> OrderProcessStatusEnums.SUCCESS.getId() == Orders.getProcessStatus()).count();
			BigDecimal sum	= value.stream().filter(Orders -> OrderProcessStatusEnums.SUCCESS.getId() == Orders.getProcessStatus()).map(MessageDto::getTotalPrice).reduce(BigDecimal.ZERO, BigDecimal::add);
			List<MessageDto> faillist = value.stream().filter(MessageDto ->  OrderProcessStatusEnums.SUCCESS.getId() != MessageDto.getProcessStatus()).collect(Collectors.toList());
			for (MessageDto o:faillist) {
				list.add(String.format("%s%s",o.getKcMessage(),o.getMobile()));
			}
			list=list.stream().distinct().collect(Collectors.toList());
			BigDecimal failCount = new BigDecimal(Integer.valueOf(list.size()));
			BigDecimal total = new BigDecimal(String.valueOf(successcount)).add(new BigDecimal(String.valueOf(failCount)));
			BigDecimal successRate =  new BigDecimal(String.valueOf(successcount)).divide(total,2,BigDecimal.ROUND_HALF_UP);
			NumberFormat percent = NumberFormat.getPercentInstance();
			percent.setMaximumFractionDigits(2);
			MessageDto messageDto =new MessageDto();
			messageDto.setProductId(map.getKey());
			messageDto.setFailcount(list.size());
			messageDto.setName(value.get(0).getName());
			messageDto.setTotalCount((int) successcount);
			messageDto.setTotalPrice(sum);
			messageDto.setSuccessRate(percent.format(successRate.doubleValue()));
			
			messageDto.setMonthTotalCount(monthCount);
			messageDtoList.add(messageDto);
		}
		List<MessageDto> sortList = messageDtoList.stream().sorted(Comparator.comparing(MessageDto::getTotalCount).reversed()).collect(Collectors.toList());
				sortList.stream().forEach(o->{
				Map map = new HashMap();
				map.put("id",o.getProductId());
				map.put("name",o.getName());
				map.put("totalCount",o.getTotalCount());
				map.put("failCount",o.getFailcount());
			   	map.put("totalPrice",o.getTotalPrice());
			   	map.put("successRate",o.getSuccessRate());
                map.put("monthTotalCount",o.getMonthTotalCount());
				res.add(map);
		});
		return res;

SELECT
	cast(`o`.`buy_time` AS date) AS `buyTime`,
	`o`.`product_id` AS `productId`,
	`o`.`customer_id` AS `customerId`,
	count(1) AS `totalCount`
FROM
	(
		`orders` `o`
		LEFT JOIN `product` `p` ON (
			(`o`.`product_id` = `p`.`id`)
		)
	)
WHERE
	(
		(`o`.`is_delete` = 0)
		AND (`o`.`is_success` = 1)
		AND (
			`p`.`type` IN (1, 2, 3, 4, 7, 8, 9)
		)
	)
GROUP BY
	cast(`o`.`buy_time` AS date),
	`o`.`product_id`,
	`o`.`customer_id`,
	`p`.`id`
ORDER BY
	cast(`o`.`buy_time` AS date) DESC,
	`o`.`product_id`,
	`o`.`customer_id`,
	`p`.`id`
	
	
	SELECT
	cast(`o`.`insert_time` AS date) AS `buyTime`,
	`o`.`product_id` AS `productId`,
	`o`.`customer_id` AS `customerId`,
	count(1) AS `totalCount`,
	sum(`o`.`price`) AS `totalPrice`
FROM
	`orders` `o`
WHERE
	(
		(`o`.`is_delete` = 0)
		AND (`o`.`is_success` = 1)
	)
GROUP BY
	cast(`o`.`insert_time` AS date),
	`o`.`product_id`,
	`o`.`customer_id`
ORDER BY
	cast(`o`.`insert_time` AS date) DESC,
	`o`.`product_id`,
	`o`.`customer_id`
